country_event = {
	id = az_tianjiang.1
	title = "来自铁血的最后通牒"
	desc = "铁血要求我们全面并入对方，我们应该怎么办？"
	picture = GFX_aze_kaixuan
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = "我莫得选择，因为我只是个小几把路人国家。"
		TIX = {
		annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = no }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "我要反抗！"
		TIX = {
		create_wargoal = { target = ROOT type = take_state_focus }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = az_tianjiang.8
	title = "遵守条约内容"
	desc = "我们应该遵守条约内容，给两边划分好领土。"
	picture = GFX_aze_luoxiya
	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = bfl_yes_pact
	NOT = {has_global_flag = bfl_yes_pact_ok}
	OR = {
	tag = TIX
	tag = BFL
	}
	country_exists = TIX
	country_exists = BFL
	TIX = {not = { has_war_with = BFL } }
	OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
				POL = { has_capitulated = yes }
				NOT = { country_exists = POL }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						BFL = {
						controls_state = 10
						}
						any_other_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = BFL
							BFL = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							controls_state = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
				POL = { has_capitulated = yes }
				NOT = { country_exists = POL }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						TIX = {
						controls_state = 10
						
						}
						any_other_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = TIX
							TIX = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							controls_state = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = "好的"
		set_global_flag = bfl_yes_pact_ok
		TIX = {
		transfer_state = 85
		transfer_state = 807
		transfer_state = 86
		transfer_state = 87
		transfer_state = 98
		transfer_state = 10
		transfer_state = 90
		transfer_state = 762
		transfer_state = 88
		transfer_state = 92
		transfer_state = 72
		transfer_state = 97
		}
		BFL = {
		transfer_state = 89
		transfer_state = 91
		transfer_state = 93
		transfer_state = 94
		transfer_state = 95
		transfer_state = 96
		transfer_state = 784
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}
